Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of LM131 revision 1, the final release of the Apollo 13 Lunar Module (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The source reconstruction began with source code of Luminary 131 previously transcribed from a digitized copy of that program. A dump of the flight spare core rope memory module B5, part number 2010802-171, serial number RAY 411, was obtained. This module is the only module different between Luminary 131 and LM131 revision 1. The dump was disassembled and all changes were incorporated into these source files. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Luminary 131 printout, although the changed code would likely have changed page numbers for a real LM131 revision 1 listing.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

016218,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
016219,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
016220,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of LM131 revision 1.
016221,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the final
016222,000006:                                                                                                  ##              release of the flight software for the Lunar Module's (LM)
016223,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13. The code has
016224,000008:                                                                                                  ##              been reconstructed from a listing of Luminary 131 and a dump
016225,000009:                                                                                                  ##              of a core rope memory module B5, part number 2010802-171,
016226,000010:                                                                                                  ##              which is the only module different between LM131 revision 1
016227,000011:                                                                                                  ##              and Luminary 131. The executable generated from this source
016228,000012:                                                                                                  ##              has been verified against the module dump, so while the names,
016229,000013:                                                                                                  ##              comments, and ordering may not be exactly correct, the
016230,000014:                                                                                                  ##              resulting binary is.
016231,000015:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 392-475
016232,000016:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
016233,000017:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
016234,000018:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
016235,000019:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2022-10-28 MAS  Created from Luminary 131.

016238,000022:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016239,000023:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016240,000024:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016241,000025:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016242,000026: 
016243,000027:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016244,000028: 
016245,000029:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016246,000030:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016247,000031:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016248,000032:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016249,000033: 
016250,000034:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016251,000035:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016252,000036:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016253,000037:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016254,000038:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016255,000039: 
016256,000040:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016257,000041:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016258,000042:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016259,000043:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016260,000044: 
016261,000045:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016262,000046:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016263,000047: 
016264,000048:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016265,000049: 
016266,000050:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016267,000051:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016268,000052:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016269,000053:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016270,000054:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016271,000055: 
016272,000056:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016273,000057:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016274,000058:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016275,000059:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016276,000060: 
016277,000061:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016278,000062:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016279,000063:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016280,000064:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016281,000065:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016282,000066: 
016283,000067:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016284,000068: 
016285,000069:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016286,000070:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016287,000071:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 393 

016289,000073:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016290,000074:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016291,000075:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016292,000076:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016293,000077:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016294,000078:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016295,000079:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016296,000080:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016297,000081:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016298,000082:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016299,000083: 
016300,000084:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016301,000085:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016302,000086:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016303,000087: 
016304,000088:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
016305,000089: 
016306,000090:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016307,000091:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016308,000092:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
016309,000093: 
016310,000094:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016311,000095:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016312,000096:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016313,000097:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016314,000098:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016315,000099:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016316,000100:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016317,000101: 
016318,000102:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016319,000103:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016320,000104: 
016321,000105:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
016322,000106: 
016323,000107:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
016324,000108:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016325,000109:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016326,000110:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016327,000111: 
016328,000112:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
016329,000113: 
016330,000114:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016331,000115:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016332,000116:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016333,000117:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016334,000118: 
016335,000119:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 394 

016337,000121:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016338,000122: 
016339,000123:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
016340,000124: 
016341,000125:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016342,000126:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
016343,000127: 
016344,000128:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016345,000129:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016346,000130:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016347,000131:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016348,000132: 
016349,000133:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
016350,000134:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016351,000135: 
016352,000136:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016353,000137:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016354,000138:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016355,000139:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016356,000140: 
016357,000141:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016358,000142:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016359,000143: 
016360,000144:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016361,000145:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
016362,000146: 
016363,000147:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016364,000148: 
016365,000149:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016366,000150:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016367,000151:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
016368,000152:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016369,000153: 
016370,000154:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016371,000155:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016372,000156: 
016373,000157:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
016374,000158:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
016375,000159: 
016376,000160:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016377,000161:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016378,000162:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016379,000163: 
016380,000164:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
016381,000165: 
016382,000166:                                                                                                  #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
016383,000167:                                                                                                  #        USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Page 395 

016385,000169:                                                                                                  #        CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
016386,000170:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
016387,000171: 
016388,000172:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016389,000173: 
016390,000174: 
016391,000175:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016392,000176:

016394,000178:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016395,000179:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   VERB CODE
016396,000180:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   NOUN CODE
016397,000181:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
016398,000182:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
016399,000183:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
016400,000184:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016401,000185:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016402,000186:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016403,000187:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016404,000188:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016405,000189:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016406,000190:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.

016408,000192:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016409,000193:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016410,000194:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016411,000195:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
016412,000196:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB

016414,000198:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)

016416,000200:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016417,000201:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER. 11-13, C RELAYS
016418,000202:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
016419,000203:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016420,000204:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
016421,000205:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016422,000206:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
016423,000207:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016424,000208:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016425,000209:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016426,000210:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016427,000211:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)

016515,000299: 
016516,000300:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
016517,000301:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
016518,000302:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
016519,000303: 
016520,000304:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016521,000305: 
016522,000306:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016523,000307: 
016524,000308:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016525,000309:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
016526,000310:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016527,000311: 
016528,000312:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016529,000313:

Page 398 

016531,000315:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016532,000316:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
016533,000317:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
016534,000318:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
016535,000319:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
016536,000320:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
016537,000321:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
016538,000322:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
016539,000323:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
016540,000324:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
016541,000325:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
016542,000326:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
016543,000327: 
016544,000328:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016545,000329:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016546,000330:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016547,000331:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016548,000332:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
016549,000333:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016550,000334: 
016551,000335:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016552,000336:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
016553,000337:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
016554,000338:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
016555,000339:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
016556,000340:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
016557,000341: 
016558,000342:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016559,000343: 
016560,000344:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016561,000345:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
016562,000346:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
016563,000347:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
016564,000348:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
016565,000349:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
016566,000350:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
016567,000351:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
016568,000352:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
016569,000353:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
016570,000354:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
016571,000355: 
016572,000356:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016573,000357: 
016574,000358:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016575,000359:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
016576,000360:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016577,000361:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016578,000362:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016579,000363:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 399 

016581,000365:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016582,000366:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016583,000367:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016584,000368:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016585,000369:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016586,000370:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016587,000371:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016588,000372:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
016589,000373: 
016590,000374:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016591,000375: 
016592,000376:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
016593,000377:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
016594,000378:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
016595,000379:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
016596,000380:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
016597,000381:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
016598,000382:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
016599,000383:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
016600,000384:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
016601,000385:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
016602,000386:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
016603,000387: 
016604,000388:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016605,000389: 
016606,000390:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016607,000391:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016608,000392:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
016609,000393:

017007,000791:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION.  HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
017008,000792:                                                                                                  #  DATA.  THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0, - FOR HIGHER
017009,000793:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.
017010,000794: 
017011,000795:                                                                                                  #  MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED (MCTBS) NOUNS DESIRE AN ECADR TO BE LOADED
017012,000796:                                                                                                  #  WHEN USED WITH LOAD VERBS, MONITOR VERBS, OR DISPLAY VERBS (EXCEPT
017013,000797:                                                                                                  #  VERB = FIXED MEMORY DISPLAY, WHICH REQUIRES AN FCADR).

Page 415 

017300,001084:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
017301,001085: 
017302,001086:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017303,001087:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
017304,001088:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017305,001089:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017306,001090:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017307,001091: 
017308,001092:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017309,001093:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017310,001094: 
017311,001095:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017312,001096: 
017313,001097:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017314,001098:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017315,001099:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017316,001100: 
017317,001101:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017318,001102:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017319,001103:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017320,001104:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017321,001105:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017322,001106:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017323,001107: 
017324,001108:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017325,001109:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017326,001110:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017327,001111:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
017328,001112:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
017329,001113: 
017330,001114:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017331,001115:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017332,001116: 
017333,001117:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017334,001118: 
017335,001119:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017336,001120:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017337,001121:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017338,001122:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017339,001123:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017340,001124: 
017341,001125:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017342,001126:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017343,001127:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017344,001128: 
017345,001129:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017346,001130:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017347,001131: 
017348,001132:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017349,001133:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
017350,001134:

Page 416

017901,001685:                                                                                                  #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOSE VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
017902,001686:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
017903,001687:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS.  IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
017904,001688:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
017905,001689:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
017906,001690:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.

Page 441 

018530,002314:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018531,002315:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018532,002316:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018533,002317:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018534,002318:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018535,002319: 
018536,002320:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018537,002321:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018538,002322:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
018539,002323:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
018540,002324:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018541,002325:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018542,002326:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018543,002327: 
018544,002328:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018545,002329:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018546,002330:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018547,002331: 
018548,002332:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018549,002333:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018550,002334: 
018551,002335:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018552,002336:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018553,002337: 
018554,002338:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

018680,002464:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018681,002465:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
018682,002466:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018683,002467:                                                                                                  #  
018684,002468:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018685,002469: 
018686,002470:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018687,002471:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018688,002472:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018689,002473: 
018690,002474:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018691,002475:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018692,002476:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018693,002477: 
018694,002478: 41,3400           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018695,002479: 41,3401           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018696,002480: 41,3402           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018697,002481: 41,3403           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018698,002482: 41,3404           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018699,002483: 41,3405           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018700,002484: 41,3406           03410                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
018701,002485: 41,3407           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019110,002894:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.

Page 454 

019112,002896: 
019113,002897:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019114,002898: 
019115,002899:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019116,002900: 
019117,002901:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019118,002902:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019119,002903:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019120,002904:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019121,002905: 
019122,002906:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019123,002907:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019124,002908:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019125,002909: 
019126,002910:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019127,002911:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019128,002912:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019129,002913:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019130,002914:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019131,002915:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019132,002916:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019133,002917:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019134,002918:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019135,002919:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019136,002920:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019137,002921: 
019138,002922: 40,3524           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019139,002923: 40,3525           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019140,002924: 40,3526           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019141,002925: 40,3527           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019142,002926: 40,3530           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019143,002927: 40,3531           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019144,002928: 40,3532           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019145,002929: 40,3533           03542                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019146,002930: 40,3534           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019147,002931: 40,3535           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019148,002932: 40,3536           03540                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019149,002933: 40,3537           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019150,002934: 40,3540           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019151,002935: 40,3541           21051                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019152,002936: 40,3542           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019153,002937: 40,3543           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019154,002938: 40,3544           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019155,002939: 40,3545           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019156,002940: 40,3546           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019157,002941: 40,3547           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019158,002942: 
019159,002943: 40,3550                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019160,002944:

Page 455 

019162,002946:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
019163,002947:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019164,002948:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019165,002949:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019166,002950:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019167,002951: 
019168,002952:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019169,002953:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
019170,002954:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019171,002955: 
019172,002956:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019173,002957:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019174,002958: 
019175,002959:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019176,002960:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019177,002961:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019178,002962:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019179,002963:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019180,002964: 
019181,002965:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019182,002966:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019183,002967:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019184,002968:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019185,002969: 
019186,002970:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019187,002971:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019188,002972:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019189,002973:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019190,002974:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019191,002975:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019192,002976:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019193,002977: 
019194,002978:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019195,002979:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019196,002980: 
019197,002981:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019198,002982:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019199,002983: 
019200,002984:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019201,002985:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019202,002986: 
019203,002987:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019204,002988:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019205,002989:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019206,002990:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019207,002991:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019208,002992:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019209,002993:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019210,002994: 
019211,002995:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 456 

019213,002997:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019214,002998:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019215,002999:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019216,003000:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019217,003001:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
019218,003002:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019219,003003:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019220,003004:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019221,003005:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019222,003006: 
019223,003007:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019224,003008:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019225,003009: 
019226,003010:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019227,003011: 
019228,003012:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN
