019336,003120:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019337,003121:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019338,003122:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019339,003123:    4205           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019340,003124:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019341,003125:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019342,003126: 
019343,003127:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
019344,003128:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019345,003129:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019346,003130:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019347,003131:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
019348,003132: 
019349,003133:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019350,003134:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019351,003135:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019352,003136:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019353,003137:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019354,003138:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019355,003139:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019356,003140:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019357,003141:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019358,003142:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
019359,003143: 
019360,003144:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 459 

019362,003146:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019363,003147:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019364,003148:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019365,003149:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019366,003150:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
019367,003151: 
019368,003152:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019369,003153:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019370,003154:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019371,003155:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
019372,003156:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019373,003157:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019374,003158:    4215           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019375,003159:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019376,003160: 
019377,003161:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019378,003162: 
019379,003163:    4220           11041        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019380,003164:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

Page 467 

019705,003489:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019706,003490: 
019707,003491:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019708,003492:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019709,003493:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019710,003494:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019711,003495: 
019712,003496:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019713,003497:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
019714,003498:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
019715,003499:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019716,003500:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019717,003501:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019718,003502:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019719,003503: 
019720,003504:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019721,003505:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019722,003506:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019723,003507:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019724,003508:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019725,003509: 
019726,003510:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019727,003511:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019728,003512:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019729,003513:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019730,003514:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019731,003515: 
019732,003516:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019733,003517:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019734,003518:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019735,003519: 
019736,003520: 
019737,003521:                                                                                                  #  .
019738,003522: 
019739,003523: 
019740,003524:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019741,003525:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019742,003526:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019743,003527:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019744,003528: 
019745,003529:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019746,003530:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019747,003531:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019748,003532: 
019749,003533:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019750,003534:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
019751,003535:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 468 

019753,003537:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019754,003538: 
019755,003539:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019756,003540:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019757,003541:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019758,003542:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019759,003543:    4443           10633                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019760,003544:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019761,003545: 
019762,003546:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019763,003547:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019764,003548: 
019765,003549: 04,2633                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019766,003550: 04,2633                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019767,003551: 04,2633           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019768,003552: 04,2634           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019769,003553: 04,2635           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019770,003554: 04,2636           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019771,003555: 04,2637           30001                           CA       L                                     
019772,003556: 04,2640           55042                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019773,003557: 04,2641           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019774,003558: 
019775,003559:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019776,003560:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019777,003561:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019778,003562:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019779,003563:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019780,003564: 
019781,003565:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019782,003566:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019783,003567:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019784,003568:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019785,003569:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019786,003570:    4450           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019787,003571:    4451           61011                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019788,003572:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019789,003573:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019790,003574:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019791,003575:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019792,003576:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019793,003577:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
019794,003578: 
019795,003579:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
019796,003580:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
019797,003581: 
019798,003582:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
019799,003583:

019949,003733:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
019950,003734:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
019951,003735:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
019952,003736: 
019953,003737:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
019954,003738:                                                                                                  #  
019955,003739:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
019956,003740:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
019957,003741:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
